## Text Elements
Fermi level is constant, throughout the structure
Wasn't there a question about this in E212? ^mQh7qEA4

Increasing energy decreases tunnelling width. ^1t87lRGP


I believe condition 2 to be the more conductive option, due to the fact that the bands have empty states in which the electrons can move in.
And through the movement of electrons we get current.
     ^Cu6H3IhD

Due to the presence of crystal potential and crystalline forces ^z2sxVGde

The motion of th electrons in a crystal can be described using the equation of classcial (Newton) physics by assigning the electron a different mass to account for the effects of the crystal potential (crystalline forces on the electron) ^Xjov54iF

Effects of the crystal potential are included in electron dynamics and the electron motion can be described using Newton's law. Note that hk is the true momentum for free electron. However, it is not the real momentum of an electron in a crystal. Therefore it is called the crystal momentum. ^lSQpj83z
